	<a class="panel-title" data-toggle="cvcollapse" data-parent="#f33ba762ar" href="#7cf709c87b">

			<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">About</h2>		</div>

				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a38f199 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="a38f199" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix"><p>Cebu Normal University was established in 1902 as a provincial normal school and a branch of the Philippine Normal School. It became an independent institution in 1924, a chartered college in 1976, and a university in 1998. It is one of the oldest educational institutions in Cebu.</p><p>CNU has three campuses, the main campus in Osmeña Boulevard, Cebu City and two extension campuses in Medellin and Balamban.</p></div>
				</div>
				</div>
